<div class="txt-block" id="name-bio-text">
        <div class="name-trivia-bio-text">
          
            <div class="inline">
    Emma Charlotte Duerre Watson was born in Paris, France, to British parents, Jacqueline Luesby and Chris Watson, both lawyers. She moved to Oxfordshire when she was five, where she attended the Dragon School. From the age of six, Emma knew that she wanted to be an actress and, for a number of years, she trained at the Oxford branch of Stagecoach ...            <span class="see-more inline nobr-only">
                    <a href="/name/nm0914612/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bio_sm"
>See full bio</a> &raquo;
            </span>
</div>        </div>
